    (ER, "ErdÅ‘s-RÃ©nyi", "blue"),
    (WS, "Watts-Strogatz", "green"),
    (BA, "BarabÃ¡si-Albert", "red"),
    (RGG, "Random Geometric", "purple")

    degrees = [d for n, d in G.degree()]
    ax.hist(degrees, bins=range(max(degrees)+2), color=color, alpha=0.7, edgecolor='black')
    ax.set_title(f"ØªÙˆØ²ÛŒØ¹ Ø¯Ø±Ø¬Ù‡ - {name}")
    ax.set_xlabel("Ø¯Ø±Ø¬Ù‡")
    ax.set_ylabel("ØªØ¹Ø¯Ø§Ø¯ Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§")

plt.tight_layout()
plt.savefig('degree_distributions.png', dpi=150)
plt.show()

import networkx as nx

# Ø§ÛŒØ¬Ø§Ø¯ Ú¯Ø±Ø§Ù Ù†Ù…ÙˆÙ†Ù‡
G = nx.Graph()
G.add_edges_from([
    ('A', 'B'), ('A', 'C'), ('B', 'D'), ('B', 'E'),
    ('C', 'F'), ('C', 'G'), ('D', 'H'), ('E', 'H'),
    ('F', 'I'), ('G', 'I'), ('H', 'J'), ('I', 'J')
])

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# Ø¬Ø³ØªØ¬ÙˆÛŒ Ø§ÙˆÙ„ Ø³Ø·Ø­ (BFS - Breadth-First Search)
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

# Ù¾ÛŒÙ…Ø§ÛŒØ´ BFS
bfs_edges = list(nx.bfs_edges(G, source='A'))
print(f"ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ BFS Ø§Ø² A: {bfs_edges}")

# Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ Ø¨Ù‡ ØªØ±ØªÛŒØ¨ BFS
bfs_nodes = list(nx.bfs_tree(G, source='A').nodes())
print(f"Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ BFS Ø§Ø² A: {bfs_nodes}")

# Ù„Ø§ÛŒÙ‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ BFS
bfs_layers = dict(enumerate(nx.bfs_layers(G, sources=['A'])))
print(f"Ù„Ø§ÛŒÙ‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ BFS: {bfs_layers}")

# Ù¾ÛŒØ´ÛŒÙ†ÛŒØ§Ù† Ø¯Ø± BFS
bfs_predecessors = dict(nx.bfs_predecessors(G, source='A'))
print(f"Ù¾ÛŒØ´ÛŒÙ†ÛŒØ§Ù† BFS: {bfs_predecessors}")

# Ø¬Ø§Ù†Ø´ÛŒÙ†Ø§Ù† Ø¯Ø± BFS
bfs_successors = dict(nx.bfs_successors(G, source='A'))
print(f"Ø¬Ø§Ù†Ø´ÛŒÙ†Ø§Ù† BFS: {bfs_successors}")

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# Ø¬Ø³ØªØ¬ÙˆÛŒ Ø§ÙˆÙ„ Ø¹Ù…Ù‚ (DFS - Depth-First Search)
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

# Ù¾ÛŒÙ…Ø§ÛŒØ´ DFS
dfs_edges = list(nx.dfs_edges(G, source='A'))
print(f"\nÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ DFS Ø§Ø² A: {dfs_edges}")

# Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ Ø¨Ù‡ ØªØ±ØªÛŒØ¨ DFS
dfs_nodes = list(nx.dfs_preorder_nodes(G, source='A'))
print(f"Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ DFS (preorder): {dfs_nodes}")

# DFS postorder
dfs_postorder = list(nx.dfs_postorder_nodes(G, source='A'))
print(f"Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ DFS (postorder): {dfs_postorder}")

# Ø¯Ø±Ø®Øª DFS
dfs_tree = nx.dfs_tree(G, source='A')
print(f"ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ø¯Ø±Ø®Øª DFS: {list(dfs_tree.edges())}")

# Ù¾ÛŒØ´ÛŒÙ†ÛŒØ§Ù† Ø¯Ø± DFS
dfs_predecessors = dict(nx.dfs_predecessors(G, source='A'))
print(f"Ù¾ÛŒØ´ÛŒÙ†ÛŒØ§Ù† DFS: {dfs_predecessors}")

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ø¨Ø±Ú¯Ø´ØªÛŒ (Back Edges)
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

# ØªØ´Ø®ÛŒØµ ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ø¨Ø±Ú¯Ø´ØªÛŒ Ø¯Ø± DFS
def find_back_edges(G, source):
    """Ù¾ÛŒØ¯Ø§ Ú©Ø±Ø¯Ù† ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ø¨Ø±Ú¯Ø´ØªÛŒ"""
    dfs_tree_edges = set(nx.dfs_edges(G, source=source))
    all_edges = set(G.edges())
    back_edges = all_edges - dfs_tree_edges - {(v, u) for u, v in dfs_tree_edges}
    return back_edges

back_edges = find_back_edges(G, 'A')
print(f"\nÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ø¨Ø±Ú¯Ø´ØªÛŒ: {back_edges}")

import networkx as nx
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

# Ø§ÛŒØ¬Ø§Ø¯ Ú¯Ø±Ø§Ù ÙˆØ²Ù†â€ŒØ¯Ø§Ø±
G = nx.Graph()
G.add_weighted_edges_from([
    ('A', 'B', 4), ('A', 'C', 2), ('B', 'C', 1),
    ('B', 'D', 5), ('C', 'D', 8), ('C', 'E', 10),
    ('D', 'E', 2), ('D', 'F', 6), ('E', 'F', 3)
])

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# Ø¯Ø±Ø®Øª Ù¾ÙˆØ´Ø§ÛŒ Ú©Ù…ÛŒÙ†Ù‡ (MST)
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

# Ø§Ù„Ú¯ÙˆØ±ÛŒØªÙ… Kruskal (Ù¾ÛŒØ´â€ŒÙØ±Ø¶)
mst_kruskal = nx.minimum_spanning_tree(G, algorithm='kruskal')
print(f"MST (Kruskal) - ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§: {list(mst_kruskal.edges(data=True))}")

# Ø§Ù„Ú¯ÙˆØ±ÛŒØªÙ… Prim

print(f"MST (Prim) - ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§: {list(mst_prim.edges(data=True))}")

# Ø§Ù„Ú¯ÙˆØ±ÛŒØªÙ… Boruvka

print(f"MST (Boruvka) - ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§: {list(mst_boruvka.edges(data=True))}")

# ÙˆØ²Ù† Ú©Ù„ MST

print(f"\nÙˆØ²Ù† Ú©Ù„ MST: {mst_weight}")

    (1, 2), (2, 3), (3, 1),  # Ù…Ø¤Ù„ÙÙ‡ Ù‚ÙˆÛŒ 1
    (4, 5), (5, 4),          # Ù…Ø¤Ù„ÙÙ‡ Ù‚ÙˆÛŒ 2
    (3, 4),                   # ÛŒØ§Ù„ Ø¨ÛŒÙ† Ù…Ø¤Ù„ÙÙ‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§
    (6, 7)                    # Ù…Ø¤Ù„ÙÙ‡ Ù‚ÙˆÛŒ 3

# Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ Ùˆ ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ø¨Ø­Ø±Ø§Ù†ÛŒ
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

G2 = nx.Graph()

    (1, 2), (2, 3), (3, 1),  # Ù…Ø«Ù„Ø«

clustering_community.py 
import networkx as nx
from networkx.algorithms import community
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt

G = nx.karate_club_graph()

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# Ø¶Ø±ÛŒØ¨ Ø®ÙˆØ´Ù‡â€ŒØ¨Ù†Ø¯ÛŒ (Clustering Coefficient)
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

# Ø¶Ø±ÛŒØ¨ Ø®ÙˆØ´Ù‡â€ŒØ¨Ù†Ø¯ÛŒ Ù‡Ø± Ú¯Ø±Ù‡
clustering = nx.clustering(G)
print("Ø¶Ø±ÛŒØ¨ Ø®ÙˆØ´Ù‡â€ŒØ¨Ù†Ø¯ÛŒ (5 Ø¨Ø±ØªØ±):")
for node, cc in sorted(clustering.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)[:5]:
    print(f"  Ú¯Ø±Ù‡ {node}: {cc:.4f}")

# Ù…ÛŒØ§Ù†Ú¯ÛŒÙ† Ø¶Ø±ÛŒØ¨ Ø®ÙˆØ´Ù‡â€ŒØ¨Ù†Ø¯ÛŒ
avg_clustering = nx.average_clustering(G)
print(f"\nÙ…ÛŒØ§Ù†Ú¯ÛŒÙ† Ø¶Ø±ÛŒØ¨ Ø®ÙˆØ´Ù‡â€ŒØ¨Ù†Ø¯ÛŒ: {avg_clustering:.4f}")

# Ø¶Ø±ÛŒØ¨ Ø®ÙˆØ´Ù‡â€ŒØ¨Ù†Ø¯ÛŒ Ú©Ù„ÛŒ (Transitivity)
transitivity = nx.transitivity(G)
print(f"Transitivity: {transitivity:.4f}")

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# ØªØ´Ø®ÛŒØµ Ø¬Ø§Ù…Ø¹Ù‡ (Community Detection)
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

# Ø§Ù„Ú¯ÙˆØ±ÛŒØªÙ… Louvain
louvain_communities = community.louvain_communities(G, seed=42)
print(f"\nØ¬ÙˆØ§Ù…Ø¹ Louvain ({len(louvain_communities)} Ø¬Ø§Ù…Ø¹Ù‡):")
for i, comm in enumerate(louvain_communities):
    print(f"  Ø¬Ø§Ù…Ø¹Ù‡ {i+1}: {sorted(comm)}")

# Ø§Ù„Ú¯ÙˆØ±ÛŒØªÙ… Girvan-Newman
gn_communities = community.girvan_newman(G)
first_level = next(gn_communities)
print(f"\nØ¬ÙˆØ§Ù…Ø¹ Girvan-Newman (Ø³Ø·Ø­ Ø§ÙˆÙ„): {[sorted(c) for c in first_level]}")

# Ø§Ù„Ú¯ÙˆØ±ÛŒØªÙ… Label Propagation
lp_communities = community.label_propagation_communities(G)
print(f"\nØ¬ÙˆØ§Ù…Ø¹ Label Propagation: {[sorted(c) for c in lp_communities]}")

# Ø§Ù„Ú¯ÙˆØ±ÛŒØªÙ… Greedy Modularity
gm_communities = community.greedy_modularity_communities(G)
print(f"\nØ¬ÙˆØ§Ù…Ø¹ Greedy Modularity: {[sorted(c) for c in gm_communities]}")

# Ø§Ù„Ú¯ÙˆØ±ÛŒØªÙ… Kernighan-Lin (Ø¨Ø±Ø§ÛŒ Ø¯Ùˆ Ø¨Ø®Ø´)
kl_partition = community.kernighan_lin_bisection(G, seed=42)
print(f"\nØªÙ‚Ø³ÛŒÙ… Kernighan-Lin: {[sorted(p) for p in kl_partition]}")

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# Modularity (Ú©ÛŒÙÛŒØª ØªÙ‚Ø³ÛŒÙ…â€ŒØ¨Ù†Ø¯ÛŒ)
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

modularity_louvain = community.modularity(G, louvain_communities)
print(f"\nModularity (Louvain): {modularity_louvain:.4f}")

modularity_gm = community.modularity(G, gm_communities)
print(f"Modularity (Greedy): {modularity_gm:.4f}")

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# k-Clique Communities
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

# Ø¬ÙˆØ§Ù…Ø¹ Ø¨Ø± Ø§Ø³Ø§Ø³ Ú©Ù„ÛŒÚ©â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ k ØªØ§ÛŒÛŒ
k_clique_comms = list(community.k_clique_communities(G, k=3))
print(f"\n3-Clique Communities: {[sorted(c) for c in k_clique_comms]}")

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# Ø±Ø³Ù… Ú¯Ø±Ø§Ù Ø¨Ø§ Ø¬ÙˆØ§Ù…Ø¹
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

plt.figure(figsize=(12, 8))

# Ø§ÛŒØ¬Ø§Ø¯ Ù†Ù‚Ø´Ù‡ Ø±Ù†Ú¯ Ø¨Ø±Ø§ÛŒ Ø¬ÙˆØ§Ù…Ø¹
node_colors = []
color_map = plt.cm.Set3(range(len(louvain_communities)))
for node in G.nodes():
    for i, comm in enumerate(louvain_communities):
        if node in comm:
            node_colors.append(color_map[i])
            break

pos = nx.spring_layout(G, seed=42)
nx.draw(G, pos, node_color=node_colors, with_labels=True,
        node_size=500, font_size=10, font_weight='bold')
plt.title(f"Karate Club - Louvain Communities (Modularity: {modularity_louvain:.3f})")
plt.savefig('community_detection.png', dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')
plt.show()

def network_summary(G):
    """Ø®Ù„Ø§ØµÙ‡ Ú©Ø§Ù…Ù„ Ù…Ø¹ÛŒØ§Ø±Ù‡Ø§ÛŒ Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡"""
    summary = {
        'nodes': G.number_of_nodes(),
        'edges': G.number_of_edges(),
        'density': nx.density(G),
        'avg_degree': sum(dict(G.degree()).values()) / G.number_of_nodes(),
        'avg_clustering': nx.average_clustering(G),
        'transitivity': nx.transitivity(G),
        'diameter': nx.diameter(G) if nx.is_connected(G) else None,
        'avg_path_length': nx.average_shortest_path_length(G) if nx.is_connected(G) else None,
        'degree_assortativity': nx.degree_assortativity_coefficient(G),
    }
    return summary

print("\n" + "=" * 50)
print("Ø®Ù„Ø§ØµÙ‡ Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡")
print("=" * 50)
for key, value in network_summary(G).items():
    if value is not None:
        print(f"{key}: {value:.4f}" if isinstance(value, float) else f"{key}: {value}")

# Ø§ÛŒØ¬Ø§Ø¯ Ú¯Ø±Ø§Ù Ù†Ù…ÙˆÙ†Ù‡
G = nx.karate_club_graph()

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

    (nx.spring_layout, "Spring Layout"),
    (nx.circular_layout, "Circular Layout"),
    (nx.kamada_kawai_layout, "Kamada-Kawai Layout"),
    (nx.shell_layout, "Shell Layout"),
    (nx.spectral_layout, "Spectral Layout"),
    (nx.random_layout, "Random Layout")
]

    if layout_func == nx.spring_layout:
        pos = layout_func(G, seed=42)
    elif layout_func == nx.random_layout:
        pos = layout_func(G, seed=42)
    else:
        pos = layout_func(G)
    
    nx.draw(G, pos, ax=ax, with_labels=True, node_color='lightblue',
            node_size=300, font_size=8)
    ax.set_title(title)

    plt.axhline(y=cumsum - 0.5, color='red', linewidth=2)
    plt.axvline(x=cumsum - 0.5, color='red', linewidth=2)

# ØªÙˆØ²ÛŒØ¹ Ø¯Ø±Ø¬Ù‡
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

                label=f'Ù…ÛŒØ§Ù†Ú¯ÛŒÙ†: {np.mean(degrees):.2f}')
axes[0].legend()

# ØªÙˆØ²ÛŒØ¹ ØªØ¬Ù…Ø¹ÛŒ Ø¯Ø±Ø¬Ù‡ (CCDF)
degree_count = {}
for d in degrees:
    degree_count[d] = degree_count.get(d, 0) + 1

sorted_degrees = sorted(degree_count.keys())
ccdf = []
total = len(degrees)
cumsum = 0
for d in sorted_degrees:
    cumsum += degree_count[d]
    ccdf.append(1 - cumsum/total)

axes[1].loglog(sorted_degrees, [degree_count[d]/total for d in sorted_degrees], 
               'bo-', label='PDF')
axes[1].set_xlabel('Ø¯Ø±Ø¬Ù‡ (log)')
axes[1].set_ylabel('Ø§Ø­ØªÙ…Ø§Ù„ (log)')
axes[1].set_title('ØªÙˆØ²ÛŒØ¹ Ø¯Ø±Ø¬Ù‡ (Ù…Ù‚ÛŒØ§Ø³ Ù„Ú¯Ø§Ø±ÛŒØªÙ…ÛŒ)')
axes[1].legend()
axes[1].grid(True, alpha=0.3)

plt.tight_layout()
plt.savefig('degree_distribution.png', dpi=150)
plt.show()

"""
Ù…ØµÙˆØ±Ø³Ø§Ø²ÛŒ ØªØ¹Ø§Ù…Ù„ÛŒ Ø¨Ø§ Pyvis
pip install pyvis

import networkx as nx
from pyvis.network import Network
from networkx.algorithms import community

# Ø§ÛŒØ¬Ø§Ø¯ Ú¯Ø±Ø§Ù
G = nx.karate_club_graph()

# ØªØ´Ø®ÛŒØµ Ø¬ÙˆØ§Ù…Ø¹
communities = community.louvain_communities(G, seed=42)

# Ø§ÛŒØ¬Ø§Ø¯ Ù†Ù‚Ø´Ù‡ Ø±Ù†Ú¯ Ø¨Ø±Ø§ÛŒ Ø¬ÙˆØ§Ù…Ø¹
colors = ['#e41a1c', '#377eb8', '#4daf4a', '#984ea3', '#ff7f00']
node_colors = {}
for i, comm in enumerate(communities):
    for node in comm:
        node_colors[node] = colors[i % len(colors)]

# Ù…Ø­Ø§Ø³Ø¨Ù‡ Ù…Ø±Ú©Ø²ÛŒØª Ø¨Ø±Ø§ÛŒ Ø§Ù†Ø¯Ø§Ø²Ù‡ Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§
betweenness = nx.betweenness_centrality(G)

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# Ø§ÛŒØ¬Ø§Ø¯ Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡ Pyvis
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

net = Network(height='700px', width='100%', bgcolor='#222222', 
              font_color='white', notebook=True)

# ØªÙ†Ø¸ÛŒÙ…Ø§Øª ÙÛŒØ²ÛŒÚ©
net.barnes_hut(gravity=-80000, central_gravity=0.3, 
               spring_length=200, spring_strength=0.001)

# Ø§Ø¶Ø§ÙÙ‡ Ú©Ø±Ø¯Ù† Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§
for node in G.nodes():
    size = 20 + betweenness[node] * 100
    net.add_node(node, 
                 label=str(node),
                 color=node_colors[node],
                 size=size,
                 title=f"Ú¯Ø±Ù‡ {node}\nØ¯Ø±Ø¬Ù‡: {G.degree(node)}\nÙ…Ø±Ú©Ø²ÛŒØª: {betweenness[node]:.3f}")

# Ø§Ø¶Ø§ÙÙ‡ Ú©Ø±Ø¯Ù† ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§
for edge in G.edges():
    net.add_edge(edge[0], edge[1])

# ØªÙ†Ø¸ÛŒÙ…Ø§Øª Ù†Ù…Ø§ÛŒØ´
net.set_options('''
var options = {
  "nodes": {
    "borderWidth": 2,
    "borderWidthSelected": 4,
    "font": {
      "size": 14,
      "face": "Tahoma"
    }
  },
  "edges": {
    "color": {
      "inherit": true
    },
    "smooth": {
      "type": "continuous"
    }
  },
  "physics": {
    "forceAtlas2Based": {
      "gravitationalConstant": -50,
      "centralGravity": 0.01,
      "springLength": 100,
      "springConstant": 0.08
    },
    "minVelocity": 0.75,
    "solver": "forceAtlas2Based"
  }
}
''')

# Ø°Ø®ÛŒØ±Ù‡ Ø¨Ù‡ ÙØ§ÛŒÙ„ HTML
net.save_graph('interactive_karate_club.html')
print("ÙØ§ÛŒÙ„ interactive_karate_club.html Ø°Ø®ÛŒØ±Ù‡ Ø´Ø¯!")

"""
Ù…ØµÙˆØ±Ø³Ø§Ø²ÛŒ ØªØ¹Ø§Ù…Ù„ÛŒ Ø¨Ø§ Plotly

"""

import networkx as nx
import plotly.graph_objects as go
from networkx.algorithms import community
import numpy as np

G = nx.karate_club_graph()

# Ù…Ø­Ø§Ø³Ø¨Ù‡ layout
pos = nx.spring_layout(G, seed=42)

# ØªØ´Ø®ÛŒØµ Ø¬ÙˆØ§Ù…Ø¹

    for node in comm:
        node_community[node] = i

# Ù…Ø­Ø§Ø³Ø¨Ù‡ Ù…Ø±Ú©Ø²ÛŒØª

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# Ø¢Ù…Ø§Ø¯Ù‡â€ŒØ³Ø§Ø²ÛŒ Ø¯Ø§Ø¯Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ Ø¨Ø±Ø§ÛŒ Plotly
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

# ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§
edge_x = []
edge_y = []
for edge in G.edges():
    x0, y0 = pos[edge[0]]
    x1, y1 = pos[edge[1]]
    edge_x.extend([x0, x1, None])
    edge_y.extend([y0, y1, None])

edge_trace = go.Scatter(
    x=edge_x, y=edge_y,
    line=dict(width=0.5, color='#888'),
    hoverinfo='none',
    mode='lines'
)

# Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§
node_x = [pos[node][0] for node in G.nodes()]
node_y = [pos[node][1] for node in G.nodes()]

# Ø±Ù†Ú¯ Ùˆ Ø§Ù†Ø¯Ø§Ø²Ù‡
node_colors = [node_community[node] for node in G.nodes()]

# Ù…ØªÙ† hover

    text = f"Ú¯Ø±Ù‡: {node}
"
    text += f"Ø¯Ø±Ø¬Ù‡: {G.degree(node)}
"
    text += f"Ø¬Ø§Ù…Ø¹Ù‡: {node_community[node]}
"
    text += f"Ù…Ø±Ú©Ø²ÛŒØª: {betweenness[node]:.3f}"
    node_text.append(text)

node_trace = go.Scatter(
    x=node_x, y=node_y,
    mode='markers+text',
    hoverinfo='text',
    text=[str(n) for n in G.nodes()],
    textposition='top center',
    hovertext=node_text,
    marker=dict(
        showscale=True,
        colorscale='Viridis',
        color=node_colors,
        size=node_sizes,
        colorbar=dict(
            thickness=15,
            title='Ø¬Ø§Ù…Ø¹Ù‡',
            xanchor='left',
            titleside='right'
        ),
        line=dict(width=2, color='white')
    )
)

                layout=go.Layout(

network_flow.py 
import networkx as nx

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# Ø¨ÛŒØ´ÛŒÙ†Ù‡ Ø¬Ø±ÛŒØ§Ù† (Maximum Flow)
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

# Ø§ÛŒØ¬Ø§Ø¯ Ú¯Ø±Ø§Ù Ø¬Ø±ÛŒØ§Ù†
G = nx.DiGraph()
G.add_edge('s', 'a', capacity=10)
G.add_edge('s', 'b', capacity=5)
G.add_edge('a', 'b', capacity=15)
G.add_edge('a', 'c', capacity=9)
G.add_edge('a', 'd', capacity=4)
G.add_edge('b', 'd', capacity=8)
G.add_edge('c', 't', capacity=10)
G.add_edge('d', 'c', capacity=15)
G.add_edge('d', 't', capacity=10)

# Ù…Ø­Ø§Ø³Ø¨Ù‡ Ø¨ÛŒØ´ÛŒÙ†Ù‡ Ø¬Ø±ÛŒØ§Ù†
flow_value, flow_dict = nx.maximum_flow(G, 's', 't')
print(f"Ø¨ÛŒØ´ÛŒÙ†Ù‡ Ø¬Ø±ÛŒØ§Ù†: {flow_value}")
print(f"Ø¬Ø±ÛŒØ§Ù† Ø¯Ø± Ù‡Ø± ÛŒØ§Ù„: {flow_dict}")

# Ø§Ù„Ú¯ÙˆØ±ÛŒØªÙ…â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ù…Ø®ØªÙ„Ù
flow_ef = nx.maximum_flow(G, 's', 't', flow_func=nx.algorithms.flow.edmonds_karp)
flow_pr = nx.maximum_flow(G, 's', 't', flow_func=nx.algorithms.flow.preflow_push)
flow_ds = nx.maximum_flow(G, 's', 't', flow_func=nx.algorithms.flow.dinitz)

print(f"\nEdmonds-Karp: {flow_ef[0]}")
print(f"Preflow-Push: {flow_pr[0]}")
print(f"Dinitz: {flow_ds[0]}")

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# Ú©Ù…ÛŒÙ†Ù‡ Ø¨Ø±Ø´ (Minimum Cut)
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

cut_value, partition = nx.minimum_cut(G, 's', 't')
reachable, non_reachable = partition
print(f"\nÚ©Ù…ÛŒÙ†Ù‡ Ø¨Ø±Ø´: {cut_value}")
print(f"Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ù‚Ø§Ø¨Ù„ Ø¯Ø³ØªØ±Ø³ Ø§Ø² s: {reachable}")
print(f"Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ ØºÛŒØ±Ù‚Ø§Ø¨Ù„ Ø¯Ø³ØªØ±Ø³: {non_reachable}")

# ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ø¨Ø±Ø´
cut_edges = []
for u in reachable:
    for v in non_reachable:
        if G.has_edge(u, v):
            cut_edges.append((u, v, G[u][v]['capacity']))
print(f"ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ø¨Ø±Ø´: {cut_edges}")

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# Ø¬Ø±ÛŒØ§Ù† Ø¨Ø§ Ú©Ù…ØªØ±ÛŒÙ† Ù‡Ø²ÛŒÙ†Ù‡ (Minimum Cost Flow)
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

MCF = nx.DiGraph()
MCF.add_edge('s', 'a', capacity=10, weight=2)
MCF.add_edge('s', 'b', capacity=5, weight=4)
MCF.add_edge('a', 'c', capacity=9, weight=3)
MCF.add_edge('b', 'c', capacity=8, weight=1)
MCF.add_edge('c', 't', capacity=20, weight=2)

# ØªØ¹ÛŒÛŒÙ† Ø¹Ø±Ø¶Ù‡ Ùˆ ØªÙ‚Ø§Ø¶Ø§
MCF.nodes['s']['demand'] = -10  # Ù…Ù†Ø¨Ø¹ (Ø¹Ø±Ø¶Ù‡)
MCF.nodes['t']['demand'] = 10   # Ù…Ù‚ØµØ¯ (ØªÙ‚Ø§Ø¶Ø§)
MCF.nodes['a']['demand'] = 0
MCF.nodes['b']['demand'] = 0
MCF.nodes['c']['demand'] = 0

# Ù…Ø­Ø§Ø³Ø¨Ù‡ Ø¬Ø±ÛŒØ§Ù† Ø¨Ø§ Ú©Ù…ØªØ±ÛŒÙ† Ù‡Ø²ÛŒÙ†Ù‡
try:
    cost, flow = nx.network_simplex(MCF)
    print(f"\nÚ©Ù…ØªØ±ÛŒÙ† Ù‡Ø²ÛŒÙ†Ù‡ Ø¬Ø±ÛŒØ§Ù†: {cost}")
    print(f"Ø¬Ø±ÛŒØ§Ù†: {flow}")
except nx.NetworkXUnfeasible:
    print("Ø¬Ø±ÛŒØ§Ù† Ø§Ù…Ú©Ø§Ù†â€ŒÙ¾Ø°ÛŒØ± Ù†ÛŒØ³Øª")

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# ØªØ·Ø§Ø¨Ù‚ (Matching)
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

# Ú¯Ø±Ø§Ù Ø¯ÙˆØ¨Ø®Ø´ÛŒ
B = nx.Graph()
B.add_nodes_from(['w1', 'w2', 'w3'], bipartite=0)  # Ú©Ø§Ø±Ú¯Ø±Ø§Ù†
B.add_nodes_from(['j1', 'j2', 'j3'], bipartite=1)  # Ú©Ø§Ø±Ù‡Ø§
B.add_edges_from([
    ('w1', 'j1'), ('w1', 'j2'),
    ('w2', 'j1'), ('w2', 'j3'),
    ('w3', 'j2'), ('w3', 'j3')
])

# Ø¨ÛŒØ´ÛŒÙ†Ù‡ ØªØ·Ø§Ø¨Ù‚
matching = nx.bipartite.maximum_matching(B)
print(f"\nØ¨ÛŒØ´ÛŒÙ†Ù‡ ØªØ·Ø§Ø¨Ù‚: {matching}")

# ØªØ·Ø§Ø¨Ù‚ Ú©Ø§Ù…Ù„ØŸ
is_perfect = len(matching) == B.number_of_nodes()
print(f"ØªØ·Ø§Ø¨Ù‚ Ú©Ø§Ù…Ù„: {is_perfect}")

ğŸ”— Ù¾ÛŒØ´â€ŒØ¨ÛŒÙ†ÛŒ Ù„ÛŒÙ†Ú© (Link Prediction)

link_prediction.py 
import networkx as nx
from networkx.algorithms import link_prediction
import pandas as pd

G = nx.karate_club_graph()

# Ø­Ø°Ù Ø¨Ø±Ø®ÛŒ ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ Ø¨Ø±Ø§ÛŒ ØªØ³Øª
test_edges = [(0, 31), (2, 32), (1, 30)]
G_train = G.copy()
G_train.remove_edges_from(test_edges)

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# Ø±ÙˆØ´â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ù¾ÛŒØ´â€ŒØ¨ÛŒÙ†ÛŒ Ù„ÛŒÙ†Ú©
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

# Ù‡Ù…Ø³Ø§ÛŒÚ¯Ø§Ù† Ù…Ø´ØªØ±Ú© (Common Neighbors)
cn_preds = list(nx.common_neighbor_centrality(G_train, test_edges))
print("Common Neighbors:")
for u, v, score in cn_preds:
    print(f"  ({u}, {v}): {score:.4f}")

# Jaccard Coefficient
jaccard_preds = list(nx.jaccard_coefficient(G_train, test_edges))
print("\nJaccard Coefficient:")
for u, v, score in jaccard_preds:
    print(f"  ({u}, {v}): {score:.4f}")

# Adamic-Adar Index
aa_preds = list(nx.adamic_adar_index(G_train, test_edges))
print("\nAdamic-Adar Index:")
for u, v, score in aa_preds:
    print(f"  ({u}, {v}): {score:.4f}")

# Preferential Attachment
pa_preds = list(nx.preferential_attachment(G_train, test_edges))
print("\nPreferential Attachment:")
for u, v, score in pa_preds:
    print(f"  ({u}, {v}): {score}")

# Resource Allocation Index
ra_preds = list(nx.resource_allocation_index(G_train, test_edges))
print("\nResource Allocation Index:")
for u, v, score in ra_preds:
    print(f"  ({u}, {v}): {score:.4f}")

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# Ù¾ÛŒØ´â€ŒØ¨ÛŒÙ†ÛŒ Ù‡Ù…Ù‡ Ù„ÛŒÙ†Ú©â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ù…Ù…Ú©Ù†
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

# Ù‡Ù…Ù‡ Ø¬ÙØªâ€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ ØºÛŒØ± Ù…ØªØµÙ„
non_edges = list(nx.non_edges(G_train))

# Ù…Ø­Ø§Ø³Ø¨Ù‡ Ø§Ù…ØªÛŒØ§Ø² Ø¨Ø±Ø§ÛŒ Ù‡Ù…Ù‡
all_predictions = []
for u, v, score in nx.adamic_adar_index(G_train, non_edges):
    all_predictions.append({'source': u, 'target': v, 'score': score})

# Ù…Ø±ØªØ¨â€ŒØ³Ø§Ø²ÛŒ Ùˆ Ù†Ù…Ø§ÛŒØ´ Ø¨Ø±ØªØ±ÛŒÙ†â€ŒÙ‡Ø§
df = pd.DataFrame(all_predictions)
df_sorted = df.sort_values('score', ascending=False)
print("\n10 Ù„ÛŒÙ†Ú© Ù¾ÛŒØ´â€ŒØ¨ÛŒÙ†ÛŒ Ø´Ø¯Ù‡ Ø¨Ø±ØªØ± (Adamic-Adar):")
print(df_sorted.head(10))

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# Ø§Ø±Ø²ÛŒØ§Ø¨ÛŒ Ù¾ÛŒØ´â€ŒØ¨ÛŒÙ†ÛŒ
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

def evaluate_link_prediction(G_original, G_train, predictions, k=10):
    """Ø§Ø±Ø²ÛŒØ§Ø¨ÛŒ Ù¾ÛŒØ´â€ŒØ¨ÛŒÙ†ÛŒ Ù„ÛŒÙ†Ú©"""
    # Ù„ÛŒÙ†Ú©â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ ÙˆØ§Ù‚Ø¹ÛŒ Ø­Ø°Ù Ø´Ø¯Ù‡
    true_edges = set(G_original.edges()) - set(G_train.edges())
    
    # k Ù¾ÛŒØ´â€ŒØ¨ÛŒÙ†ÛŒ Ø¨Ø±ØªØ±
    top_k = predictions.head(k)
    predicted_edges = set(zip(top_k['source'], top_k['target']))
    
    # Ù…Ø­Ø§Ø³Ø¨Ù‡ precision
    hits = len(predicted_edges & true_edges)
    precision = hits / k if k > 0 else 0
    
    return {
        'precision@k': precision,
        'hits': hits,
        'k': k
    }

eval_result = evaluate_link_prediction(G, G_train, df_sorted, k=10)
print(f"\nØ§Ø±Ø²ÛŒØ§Ø¨ÛŒ: {eval_result}")

import json

G = nx.karate_club_graph()

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# ÙØ±Ù…Øªâ€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ù…ØªÙ†ÛŒ

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

# Pickle (Ø³Ø±ÛŒØ¹â€ŒØªØ±ÛŒÙ†)
import pickle
with open('graph.pkl', 'wb') as f:
    pickle.dump(G, f)

with open('graph.pkl', 'rb') as f:
    G_pkl = pickle.load(f)

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•
# JSON
# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

from concurrent.futures import ProcessPoolExecutor, ThreadPoolExecutor
import multiprocessing

def compute_local_clustering(nodes_chunk, G):
    """Ù…Ø­Ø§Ø³Ø¨Ù‡ Ø®ÙˆØ´Ù‡â€ŒØ¨Ù†Ø¯ÛŒ Ù…Ø­Ù„ÛŒ Ø¨Ø±Ø§ÛŒ Ú¯Ø±ÙˆÙ‡ÛŒ Ø§Ø² Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§"""
    return {n: nx.clustering(G, n) for n in nodes_chunk}

def parallel_clustering(G, n_workers=4):
    """Ù…Ø­Ø§Ø³Ø¨Ù‡ Ù…ÙˆØ§Ø²ÛŒ Ø®ÙˆØ´Ù‡â€ŒØ¨Ù†Ø¯ÛŒ"""
    nodes = list(G.nodes())
    chunk_size = len(nodes) // n_workers
    chunks = [nodes[i:i+chunk_size] for i in range(0, len(nodes), chunk_size)]
    
    results = {}
    with ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=n_workers) as executor:
        futures = [executor.submit(compute_local_clustering, chunk, G) 
                   for chunk in chunks]
        for future in futures:
            results.update(future.result())
    
    return results

# ØªØ³Øª Ø¨Ø§ Ú¯Ø±Ø§Ù Ú©ÙˆÚ†Ú©â€ŒØªØ±

"""
ØªØ­Ù„ÛŒÙ„ Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡ Ø§Ø¬ØªÙ…Ø§Ø¹ÛŒ Ú©Ø§Ù…Ù„

import networkx as nx
from networkx.algorithms import community
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np

class SocialNetworkAnalyzer:
    def __init__(self, graph=None):
        self.G = graph if graph else nx.Graph()
        self.communities = None
        self.centrality_scores = {}
    
    def load_from_edges(self, edges):
        """Ø¨Ø§Ø±Ú¯Ø°Ø§Ø±ÛŒ Ø§Ø² Ù„ÛŒØ³Øª ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§"""
        self.G.add_edges_from(edges)
        return self
    
    def load_from_csv(self, filepath, source_col='source', target_col='target'):
        """Ø¨Ø§Ø±Ú¯Ø°Ø§Ø±ÛŒ Ø§Ø² ÙØ§ÛŒÙ„ CSV"""
        df = pd.read_csv(filepath)
        self.G = nx.from_pandas_edgelist(df, source_col, target_col)
        return self
    
    def basic_stats(self):
        """Ø¢Ù…Ø§Ø± Ù¾Ø§ÛŒÙ‡ Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡"""
        return {
            'nodes': self.G.number_of_nodes(),
            'edges': self.G.number_of_edges(),
            'density': nx.density(self.G),
            'avg_degree': np.mean([d for n, d in self.G.degree()]),
            'is_connected': nx.is_connected(self.G),
            'num_components': nx.number_connected_components(self.G)
        }
    
    def compute_centralities(self):
        """Ù…Ø­Ø§Ø³Ø¨Ù‡ Ù‡Ù…Ù‡ Ù…Ø¹ÛŒØ§Ø±Ù‡Ø§ÛŒ Ù…Ø±Ú©Ø²ÛŒØª"""
        self.centrality_scores = {
            'degree': nx.degree_centrality(self.G),
            'betweenness': nx.betweenness_centrality(self.G),
            'closeness': nx.closeness_centrality(self.G),
            'eigenvector': nx.eigenvector_centrality(self.G, max_iter=1000),
            'pagerank': nx.pagerank(self.G)
        }
        return self.centrality_scores
    
    def find_influencers(self, top_n=10):
        """ÛŒØ§ÙØªÙ† Ø§ÙØ±Ø§Ø¯ ØªØ£Ø«ÛŒØ±Ú¯Ø°Ø§Ø±"""
        if not self.centrality_scores:
            self.compute_centralities()
        
        # ØªØ±Ú©ÛŒØ¨ Ù…Ø¹ÛŒØ§Ø±Ù‡Ø§
        combined_score = {}
        for node in self.G.nodes():
            combined_score[node] = (
                self.centrality_scores['degree'][node] * 0.2 +
                self.centrality_scores['betweenness'][node] * 0.3 +
                self.centrality_scores['eigenvector'][node] * 0.3 +
                self.centrality_scores['pagerank'][node] * 0.2
            )
        
        # Ù…Ø±ØªØ¨â€ŒØ³Ø§Ø²ÛŒ
        sorted_nodes = sorted(combined_score.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)
        return sorted_nodes[:top_n]
def detect_communities(self, method='louvain'):
        """ØªØ´Ø®ÛŒØµ Ø¬ÙˆØ§Ù…Ø¹"""
        if method == 'louvain':
            self.communities = list(community.louvain_communities(self.G, seed=42))
        elif method == 'greedy':
            self.communities = list(community.greedy_modularity_communities(self.G))
        elif method == 'label_propagation':
            self.communities = list(community.label_propagation_communities(self.G))
        
        return self.communities
    
    def get_community_stats(self):
        """Ø¢Ù…Ø§Ø± Ø¬ÙˆØ§Ù…Ø¹"""
        if not self.communities:
            self.detect_communities()
        
        stats = {
            'num_communities': len(self.communities),
            'modularity': community.modularity(self.G, self.communities),
            'sizes': [len(c) for c in self.communities],
            'avg_size': np.mean([len(c) for c in self.communities])
        }
        return stats
    
    def find_bridges(self):
        """ÛŒØ§ÙØªÙ† Ù¾Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ø§Ø±ØªØ¨Ø§Ø·ÛŒ Ø¨ÛŒÙ† Ø¬ÙˆØ§Ù…Ø¹"""
        if not self.communities:
            self.detect_communities()
        
        # Ø§ÛŒØ¬Ø§Ø¯ Ù†Ù‚Ø´Ù‡ Ú¯Ø±Ù‡ Ø¨Ù‡ Ø¬Ø§Ù…Ø¹Ù‡
        node_to_comm = {}
        for i, comm in enumerate(self.communities):
            for node in comm:
                node_to_comm[node] = i
        
        # ÛŒØ§ÙØªÙ† ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ø¨ÛŒÙ† Ø¬ÙˆØ§Ù…Ø¹
        bridge_edges = []
        for u, v in self.G.edges():
            if node_to_comm[u] != node_to_comm[v]:
                bridge_edges.append((u, v))
        
        # Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ù¾Ù„
        bridge_nodes = set()
        for u, v in bridge_edges:
            bridge_nodes.add(u)
            bridge_nodes.add(v)
        
        return {
            'bridge_edges': bridge_edges,
            'bridge_nodes': list(bridge_nodes),
            'num_bridges': len(bridge_edges)
        }
    
    def visualize(self, highlight_communities=True, save_path=None):
        """Ù…ØµÙˆØ±Ø³Ø§Ø²ÛŒ Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡"""
        plt.figure(figsize=(14, 10))
        pos = nx.spring_layout(self.G, seed=42, k=2)
        
        if highlight_communities and self.communities:
            # Ø±Ù†Ú¯â€ŒØ¨Ù†Ø¯ÛŒ Ø¨Ø± Ø§Ø³Ø§Ø³ Ø¬Ø§Ù…Ø¹Ù‡
            colors = plt.cm.Set3(np.linspace(0, 1, len(self.communities)))
            node_colors = []
            for node in self.G.nodes():
                for i, comm in enumerate(self.communities):
                    if node in comm:
                        node_colors.append(colors[i])
                        break
        else:
            node_colors = 'lightblue'
        
        # Ø§Ù†Ø¯Ø§Ø²Ù‡ Ø¨Ø± Ø§Ø³Ø§Ø³ Ø¯Ø±Ø¬Ù‡
        degrees = dict(self.G.degree())
        node_sizes = [300 + degrees[n] * 100 for n in self.G.nodes()]
        
        nx.draw(self.G, pos, node_color=node_colors, node_size=node_sizes,
                with_labels=True, font_size=8, alpha=0.9)
        
        plt.title("Social Network Analysis")
        
        if save_path:
            plt.savefig(save_path, dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')
        
        plt.show()
    
    def generate_report(self):
        """ØªÙˆÙ„ÛŒØ¯ Ú¯Ø²Ø§Ø±Ø´ Ú©Ø§Ù…Ù„"""
        report = []
        report.append("=" * 60)
        report.append("Ú¯Ø²Ø§Ø±Ø´ ØªØ­Ù„ÛŒÙ„ Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡ Ø§Ø¬ØªÙ…Ø§Ø¹ÛŒ")
        report.append("=" * 60)
        
        # Ø¢Ù…Ø§Ø± Ù¾Ø§ÛŒÙ‡
        stats = self.basic_stats()
        report.append("\nğŸ“Š Ø¢Ù…Ø§Ø± Ù¾Ø§ÛŒÙ‡:")
        for key, value in stats.items():
            report.append(f"  {key}: {value}")
        
        # Ù…Ø±Ú©Ø²ÛŒØª
        self.compute_centralities()
        influencers = self.find_influencers(5)
        report.append("\nğŸŒŸ Ø§ÙØ±Ø§Ø¯ ØªØ£Ø«ÛŒØ±Ú¯Ø°Ø§Ø± (5 Ø¨Ø±ØªØ±):")
        for node, score in influencers:
            report.append(f"  {node}: {score:.4f}")
        
        # Ø¬ÙˆØ§Ù…Ø¹
        self.detect_communities()
        comm_stats = self.get_community_stats()
        report.append(f"\nğŸ˜ï¸ Ø¬ÙˆØ§Ù…Ø¹ ({comm_stats['num_communities']} Ø¬Ø§Ù…Ø¹Ù‡):")
        report.append(f"  Modularity: {comm_stats['modularity']:.4f}")
        report.append(f"  Ù…ÛŒØ§Ù†Ú¯ÛŒÙ† Ø§Ù†Ø¯Ø§Ø²Ù‡: {comm_stats['avg_size']:.1f}")
        
        # Ù¾Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§
        bridges = self.find_bridges()
        report.append(f"\nğŸŒ‰ Ù¾Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ø§Ø±ØªØ¨Ø§Ø·ÛŒ:")
        report.append(f"  ØªØ¹Ø¯Ø§Ø¯ ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ù¾Ù„: {bridges['num_bridges']}")
        report.append(f"  Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ù¾Ù„: {bridges['bridge_nodes'][:10]}...")
        
        return "\n".join(report)


# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

# â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•â•

"""
ØªØ­Ù„ÛŒÙ„ Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡ Ø­Ù…Ù„ Ùˆ Ù†Ù‚Ù„
"""

import networkx as nx
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
import numpy as np
from collections import defaultdict

class TransportationNetwork:
    def __init__(self):
        self.G = nx.DiGraph()
        self.stations = {}
        self.lines = defaultdict(list)
    
    def add_station(self, station_id, name, lat=None, lon=None, **attrs):
        """Ø§Ø¶Ø§ÙÙ‡ Ú©Ø±Ø¯Ù† Ø§ÛŒØ³ØªÚ¯Ø§Ù‡"""
        self.G.add_node(station_id, name=name, lat=lat, lon=lon, **attrs)
        self.stations[station_id] = name
    
    def add_connection(self, from_station, to_station, line, 
                       distance=None, time=None, **attrs):
        """Ø§Ø¶Ø§ÙÙ‡ Ú©Ø±Ø¯Ù† Ø§ØªØµØ§Ù„ Ø¨ÛŒÙ† Ø§ÛŒØ³ØªÚ¯Ø§Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§"""
        self.G.add_edge(from_station, to_station, 
                        line=line, distance=distance, time=time, **attrs)
        self.G.add_edge(to_station, from_station,
                        line=line, distance=distance, time=time, **attrs)
        
        self.lines[line].append((from_station, to_station))
    
    def shortest_path(self, origin, destination, weight='time'):
        """Ú©ÙˆØªØ§Ù‡â€ŒØªØ±ÛŒÙ† Ù…Ø³ÛŒØ±"""
        try:
            path = nx.dijkstra_path(self.G, origin, destination, weight=weight)
            length = nx.dijkstra_path_length(self.G, origin, destination, weight=weight)
            
            # Ø¬Ø²Ø¦ÛŒØ§Øª Ù…Ø³ÛŒØ±
            details = []
            for i in range(len(path) - 1):
                edge_data = self.G[path[i]][path[i+1]]
                details.append({
                    'from': self.stations.get(path[i], path[i]),
                    'to': self.stations.get(path[i+1], path[i+1]),
                    'line': edge_data.get('line'),
                    'time': edge_data.get('time'),
                    'distance': edge_data.get('distance')
                })
            
            return {
                'path': path,
                'path_names': [self.stations.get(s, s) for s in path],
                'total_length': length,
                'details': details,
                'num_stops': len(path) - 1
            }
        except nx.NetworkXNoPath:
            return None
    
    def find_all_paths(self, origin, destination, max_paths=5):
        """ÛŒØ§ÙØªÙ† Ù‡Ù…Ù‡ Ù…Ø³ÛŒØ±Ù‡Ø§ÛŒ Ù…Ù…Ú©Ù†"""
        paths = list(nx.shortest_simple_paths(self.G, origin, destination, weight='time'))
        return paths[:max_paths]
    
    def station_importance(self):
        """Ø§Ù‡Ù…ÛŒØª Ø§ÛŒØ³ØªÚ¯Ø§Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§"""
        betweenness = nx.betweenness_centrality(self.G)
        degree = dict(self.G.degree())
        
        importance = {}
        for station in self.G.nodes():
            importance[station] = {
                'name': self.stations.get(station, station),
                'betweenness': betweenness[station],
                'connections': degree[station],
                'lines': len(set(self.G[station][n].get('line') 
                               for n in self.G.neighbors(station)))
            }
        
        return importance
    
    def find_critical_stations(self):
        """Ø§ÛŒØ³ØªÚ¯Ø§Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ø­ÛŒØ§ØªÛŒ (Ø­Ø°Ù Ø¢Ù†Ù‡Ø§ Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡ Ø±Ø§ Ù‚Ø·Ø¹ Ù…ÛŒâ€ŒÚ©Ù†Ø¯)"""
        # ØªØ¨Ø¯ÛŒÙ„ Ø¨Ù‡ Ú¯Ø±Ø§Ù Ø¨Ø¯ÙˆÙ† Ø¬Ù‡Øª
        G_undirected = self.G.to_undirected()
        
        # Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ø¨Ø±Ø´ÛŒ
        articulation_points = list(nx.articulation_points(G_undirected))
        
        return [{'id': s, 'name': self.stations.get(s, s)} 
                for s in articulation_points]
    
    def network_coverage(self, max_distance=2):
        """Ù¾ÙˆØ´Ø´ Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡ Ø§Ø² Ù‡Ø± Ø§ÛŒØ³ØªÚ¯Ø§Ù‡"""
        coverage = {}
        for station in self.G.nodes():
            # Ø§ÛŒØ³ØªÚ¯Ø§Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ù‚Ø§Ø¨Ù„ Ø¯Ø³ØªØ±Ø³ Ø¯Ø± max_distance Ú¯Ø§Ù…
            reachable = nx.single_source_shortest_path_length(
                self.G, station, cutoff=max_distance
            )
            coverage[station] = {
                'name': self.stations.get(station, station),
                'reachable_count': len(reachable),
                'reachable_stations': list(reachable.keys())
            }
        return coverage
    
    def line_statistics(self):
        """Ø¢Ù…Ø§Ø± Ø®Ø·ÙˆØ·"""
        stats = {}
        for line, edges in self.lines.items():
            stations_in_line = set()
            total_distance = 0
            total_time = 0
            
            for u, v in edges:
                stations_in_line.add(u)
                stations_in_line.add(v)
                edge_data = self.G[u][v]
                if edge_data.get('distance'):
                    total_distance += edge_data['distance']
                if edge_data.get('time'):
                    total_time += edge_data['time']
            
            stats[line] = {
                'num_stations': len(stations_in_line),
                'num_connections': len(edges),
                'total_distance': total_distance,
                'total_time': total_time
            }
        
        return stats
    
    def visualize(self, highlight_path=None, save_path=None):
        """Ù…ØµÙˆØ±Ø³Ø§Ø²ÛŒ Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡"""
        plt.figure(figsize=(16, 12))
        
        # Ø§Ø³ØªÙØ§Ø¯Ù‡ Ø§Ø² Ù…ÙˆÙ‚Ø¹ÛŒØª Ø¬ØºØ±Ø§ÙÛŒØ§ÛŒÛŒ Ø§Ú¯Ø± Ù…ÙˆØ¬ÙˆØ¯ Ø§Ø³Øª
        pos = {}
        for node in self.G.nodes():
            data = self.G.nodes[node]

                pos[node] = (data['lon'], data['lat'])
        
        if not pos:
            pos = nx.spring_layout(self.G, seed=42, k=2)
        
        # Ø±Ù†Ú¯â€ŒØ¨Ù†Ø¯ÛŒ ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ Ø¨Ø± Ø§Ø³Ø§Ø³ Ø®Ø·
        line_colors = plt.cm.Set1(np.linspace(0, 1, len(self.lines)))

        edge_colors = []
        for u, v in self.G.edges():
            line = self.G[u][v].get('line', 'default')
            edge_colors.append(line_color_map.get(line, 'gray'))
        
        # Ø±Ø³Ù… ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§
        nx.draw_networkx_edges(self.G, pos, edge_color=edge_colors, 
                               width=2, alpha=0.7, arrows=False)

        importance = self.station_importance()

                               node_color='lightblue', edgecolors='black')
        
        # Ø¨Ø±Ú†Ø³Ø¨â€ŒÙ‡Ø§
        labels = {n: self.stations.get(n, n) for n in self.G.nodes()}
        nx.draw_networkx_labels(self.G, pos, labels, font_size=8)

        if highlight_path:

                         for i in range(len(highlight_path)-1)]
            nx.draw_networkx_edges(self.G, pos, edgelist=path_edges,
                                   edge_color='red', width=4, alpha=0.8)
            nx.draw_networkx_nodes(self.G, pos, nodelist=highlight_path,
                                   node_color='red', node_size=500)
        
        # Legend

            plt.plot([], [], color=color, linewidth=3, label=f'Ø®Ø· {line}')
        plt.legend(loc='upper left')
        
        plt.title("Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡ Ø­Ù…Ù„ Ùˆ Ù†Ù‚Ù„")
        plt.axis('off')
        
        if save_path:

        plt.show()

citation_network.py 
"""
ØªØ­Ù„ÛŒÙ„ Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡ Ø§Ø³ØªÙ†Ø§Ø¯ Ø¹Ù„Ù…ÛŒ
"""

import networkx as nx
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
from collections import defaultdict
import numpy as np

class CitationNetwork:
    def __init__(self):
        self.G = nx.DiGraph()  # Ú¯Ø±Ø§Ù Ø¬Ù‡Øªâ€ŒØ¯Ø§Ø± Ø¨Ø±Ø§ÛŒ Ø§Ø³ØªÙ†Ø§Ø¯Ù‡Ø§
        self.papers = {}
        self.authors = defaultdict(list)
    
    def add_paper(self, paper_id, title, authors, year, **attrs):
        """Ø§Ø¶Ø§ÙÙ‡ Ú©Ø±Ø¯Ù† Ù…Ù‚Ø§Ù„Ù‡"""
        self.G.add_node(paper_id, title=title, authors=authors, 
                        year=year, **attrs)
        self.papers[paper_id] = {
            'title': title,
            'authors': authors,
            'year': year,
            **attrs
        }
        
        # Ø§Ø¶Ø§ÙÙ‡ Ú©Ø±Ø¯Ù† Ø¨Ù‡ Ù„ÛŒØ³Øª Ù†ÙˆÛŒØ³Ù†Ø¯Ú¯Ø§Ù†
        for author in authors:
            self.authors[author].append(paper_id)
    
    def add_citation(self, citing_paper, cited_paper):
        """Ø§Ø¶Ø§ÙÙ‡ Ú©Ø±Ø¯Ù† Ø§Ø³ØªÙ†Ø§Ø¯ (citing_paper Ø¨Ù‡ cited_paper Ø§Ø±Ø¬Ø§Ø¹ Ù…ÛŒâ€ŒØ¯Ù‡Ø¯)"""
        self.G.add_edge(citing_paper, cited_paper)
    
    def citation_count(self, paper_id):
        """ØªØ¹Ø¯Ø§Ø¯ Ø§Ø³ØªÙ†Ø§Ø¯Ù‡Ø§ Ø¨Ù‡ ÛŒÚ© Ù…Ù‚Ø§Ù„Ù‡"""
        return self.G.in_degree(paper_id)
    
    def reference_count(self, paper_id):
        """ØªØ¹Ø¯Ø§Ø¯ Ø§Ø±Ø¬Ø§Ø¹Ø§Øª ÛŒÚ© Ù…Ù‚Ø§Ù„Ù‡"""
        return self.G.out_degree(paper_id)
    
    def most_cited_papers(self, top_n=10):
        """Ù¾Ø±Ø§Ø³ØªÙ†Ø§Ø¯ØªØ±ÛŒÙ† Ù…Ù‚Ø§Ù„Ø§Øª"""
        citations = [(p, self.citation_count(p)) for p in self.G.nodes()]
        sorted_papers = sorted(citations, key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)
        
        result = []
        for paper_id, count in sorted_papers[:top_n]:
            paper_data = self.papers.get(paper_id, {})
            result.append({
                'id': paper_id,
                'title': paper_data.get('title', 'Unknown'),
                'citations': count,
                'year': paper_data.get('year')
            })
        
        return result
    
    def author_impact(self):
        """ØªØ£Ø«ÛŒØ± Ù†ÙˆÛŒØ³Ù†Ø¯Ú¯Ø§Ù†"""
        impact = {}
        for author, papers in self.authors.items():
            total_citations = sum(self.citation_count(p) for p in papers)
            h_index = self._calculate_h_index(papers)
            
            impact[author] = {
                'papers': len(papers),
                'total_citations': total_citations,
                'h_index': h_index,
                'avg_citations': total_citations / len(papers) if papers else 0
            }
        
        return impact
    
    def _calculate_h_index(self, papers):
        """Ù…Ø­Ø§Ø³Ø¨Ù‡ h-index"""
        citations = sorted([self.citation_count(p) for p in papers], reverse=True)
        h = 0
        for i, c in enumerate(citations):
            if c >= i + 1:
                h = i + 1
            else:
                break
        return h
    
    def find_influential_papers(self):
        """Ù…Ù‚Ø§Ù„Ø§Øª ØªØ£Ø«ÛŒØ±Ú¯Ø°Ø§Ø± Ø¨Ø§ PageRank"""
        pagerank = nx.pagerank(self.G)
        sorted_papers = sorted(pagerank.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)
        
        result = []
        for paper_id, score in sorted_papers[:10]:
            paper_data = self.papers.get(paper_id, {})
            result.append({
                'id': paper_id,
                'title': paper_data.get('title', 'Unknown'),
                'pagerank': score,
                'citations': self.citation_count(paper_id)
            })
        
        return result
    
    def find_seminal_papers(self):
        """Ù…Ù‚Ø§Ù„Ø§Øª Ø¨Ù†ÛŒØ§Ø¯ÛŒ (Ø§Ø³ØªÙ†Ø§Ø¯ Ø¨Ø§Ù„Ø§ØŒ Ø§Ø±Ø¬Ø§Ø¹ Ú©Ù…)"""
        seminal = []
        for paper in self.G.nodes():
            in_deg = self.G.in_degree(paper)
            out_deg = self.G.out_degree(paper)
            
            if in_deg > 0 and out_deg < 5:  # Ø§Ø³ØªÙ†Ø§Ø¯ Ø¨Ø§Ù„Ø§ØŒ Ø§Ø±Ø¬Ø§Ø¹ Ú©Ù…
                ratio = in_deg / (out_deg + 1)
                seminal.append((paper, in_deg, out_deg, ratio))
        
        sorted_seminal = sorted(seminal, key=lambda x: x[3], reverse=True)
        
        return [{'id': p, 'citations': c, 'references': r, 'ratio': ratio}
                for p, c, r, ratio in sorted_seminal[:10]]
    
    def citation_network_metrics(self):
        """Ù…Ø¹ÛŒØ§Ø±Ù‡Ø§ÛŒ Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡ Ø§Ø³ØªÙ†Ø§Ø¯"""
        return {
            'total_papers': self.G.number_of_nodes(),
            'total_citations': self.G.number_of_edges(),
            'avg_citations': self.G.number_of_edges() / self.G.number_of_nodes() if self.G.number_of_nodes() > 0 else 0,
            'density': nx.density(self.G),
            'is_dag': nx.is_directed_acyclic_graph(self.G),
            'num_weakly_connected': nx.number_weakly_connected_components(self.G),
            'num_strongly_connected': nx.number_strongly_connected_components(self.G)
        }
    
    def co_citation_analysis(self, min_co_citations=2):
        """ØªØ­Ù„ÛŒÙ„ Ù‡Ù…â€ŒØ§Ø³ØªÙ†Ø§Ø¯ÛŒ"""
        co_citation = nx.Graph()

        for paper in self.G.nodes():

            for citing in citing_papers:
                co_cited = list(self.G.successors(citing))
                for co in co_cited:
                    if co != paper:
                        if co_citation.has_edge(paper, co):
                            co_citation[paper][co]['weight'] += 1
                        else:
                            co_citation.add_edge(paper, co, weight=1)
        
        # ÙÛŒÙ„ØªØ± Ø¨Ø± Ø§Ø³Ø§Ø³ Ø­Ø¯Ø§Ù‚Ù„ Ù‡Ù…â€ŒØ§Ø³ØªÙ†Ø§Ø¯ÛŒ
        edges_to_remove = [(u, v) for u, v, d in co_citation.edges(data=True) 
                          if d['weight'] < min_co_citations]
        co_citation.remove_edges_from(edges_to_remove)
        
        return co_citation
    
    def visualize(self, layout='spring', save_path=None):
        """Ù…ØµÙˆØ±Ø³Ø§Ø²ÛŒ Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡ Ø§Ø³ØªÙ†Ø§Ø¯"""
        plt.figure(figsize=(16, 12))
        
        if layout == 'spring':
            pos = nx.spring_layout(self.G, seed=42, k=2)
        elif layout == 'kamada_kawai':
            pos = nx.kamada_kawai_layout(self.G)

"""
ØªØ­Ù„ÛŒÙ„ Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡ Ø¬ØºØ±Ø§ÙÛŒØ§ÛŒÛŒ Ø¨Ø§ NetworkX Ùˆ GIS
"""

import networkx as nx
import numpy as np
import matplotlib.pyplot as plt
from math import radians, sin, cos, sqrt, atan2

class GeoNetwork:
    def __init__(self):
        self.G = nx.Graph()
    
    def add_location(self, location_id, name, lat, lon, **attrs):
        """Ø§Ø¶Ø§ÙÙ‡ Ú©Ø±Ø¯Ù† Ù…ÙˆÙ‚Ø¹ÛŒØª Ø¬ØºØ±Ø§ÙÛŒØ§ÛŒÛŒ"""
        self.G.add_node(location_id, name=name, lat=lat, lon=lon, **attrs)
    
    def add_connection(self, loc1, loc2, **attrs):
        """Ø§Ø¶Ø§ÙÙ‡ Ú©Ø±Ø¯Ù† Ø§ØªØµØ§Ù„ Ø¨Ø§ Ù…Ø­Ø§Ø³Ø¨Ù‡ ÙØ§ØµÙ„Ù‡ Ø®ÙˆØ¯Ú©Ø§Ø±"""
        # Ù…Ø­Ø§Ø³Ø¨Ù‡ ÙØ§ØµÙ„Ù‡ Ø¬ØºØ±Ø§ÙÛŒØ§ÛŒÛŒ
        distance = self._haversine_distance(loc1, loc2)
        self.G.add_edge(loc1, loc2, distance=distance, **attrs)
    
    def _haversine_distance(self, loc1, loc2):
        """Ù…Ø­Ø§Ø³Ø¨Ù‡ ÙØ§ØµÙ„Ù‡ Haversine Ø¨ÛŒÙ† Ø¯Ùˆ Ù†Ù‚Ø·Ù‡"""
        R = 6371  # Ø´Ø¹Ø§Ø¹ Ø²Ù…ÛŒÙ† Ø¨Ù‡ Ú©ÛŒÙ„ÙˆÙ…ØªØ±
        
        lat1 = radians(self.G.nodes[loc1]['lat'])
        lon1 = radians(self.G.nodes[loc1]['lon'])
        lat2 = radians(self.G.nodes[loc2]['lat'])
        lon2 = radians(self.G.nodes[loc2]['lon'])
        
        dlat = lat2 - lat1
        dlon = lon2 - lon1
        
        a = sin(dlat/2)**2 + cos(lat1) * cos(lat2) * sin(dlon/2)**2
        c = 2 * atan2(sqrt(a), sqrt(1-a))
        
        return R * c
    
    def shortest_geographic_path(self, origin, destination):
        """Ú©ÙˆØªØ§Ù‡â€ŒØªØ±ÛŒÙ† Ù…Ø³ÛŒØ± Ø¬ØºØ±Ø§ÙÛŒØ§ÛŒÛŒ"""
        try:
            path = nx.dijkstra_path(self.G, origin, destination, weight='distance')
            length = nx.dijkstra_path_length(self.G, origin, destination, weight='distance')
            
            return {
                'path': path,
                'path_names': [self.G.nodes[n]['name'] for n in path],
                'total_distance': length,
                'num_stops': len(path) - 1
            }
        except nx.NetworkXNoPath:
            return None
    
    def service_area(self, location, max_distance):
        """Ù…Ù†Ø·Ù‚Ù‡ Ø®Ø¯Ù…Ø§Øªâ€ŒØ±Ø³Ø§Ù†ÛŒ (Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ù‚Ø§Ø¨Ù„ Ø¯Ø³ØªØ±Ø³ Ø¯Ø± ÙØ§ØµÙ„Ù‡ Ù…Ø´Ø®Øµ)"""
        distances = nx.single_source_dijkstra_path_length(
            self.G, location, weight='distance'
        )
        
        reachable = {loc: dist for loc, dist in distances.items() 
                     if dist <= max_distance}
        
        return {
            'center': location,
            'center_name': self.G.nodes[location]['name'],
            'max_distance': max_distance,
            'reachable_count': len(reachable),
            'reachable_locations': reachable
        }
    
    def network_connectivity_analysis(self):
        """ØªØ­Ù„ÛŒÙ„ Ø§ØªØµØ§Ù„ Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡"""
        return {
            'is_connected': nx.is_connected(self.G),
            'num_components': nx.number_connected_components(self.G),
            'avg_clustering': nx.average_clustering(self.G),
            'diameter': nx.diameter(self.G) if nx.is_connected(self.G) else None,
            'avg_path_length': nx.average_shortest_path_length(self.G, weight='distance') 
                              if nx.is_connected(self.G) else None
        }
    
    def find_central_locations(self):
        """ÛŒØ§ÙØªÙ† Ù…ÙˆÙ‚Ø¹ÛŒØªâ€ŒÙ‡Ø§ÛŒ Ù…Ø±Ú©Ø²ÛŒ"""
        # Ù…Ø±Ú©Ø²ÛŒØª Ù†Ø²Ø¯ÛŒÚ©ÛŒ (Ø¨Ø± Ø§Ø³Ø§Ø³ ÙØ§ØµÙ„Ù‡ Ø¬ØºØ±Ø§ÙÛŒØ§ÛŒÛŒ)
        closeness = nx.closeness_centrality(self.G, distance='distance')
        
        # Ù…Ø±Ú©Ø²ÛŒØª Ø¨ÛŒÙ†Ø§Ø¨ÛŒÙ†ÛŒ
        betweenness = nx.betweenness_centrality(self.G, weight='distance')
        
        results = []
        for loc in self.G.nodes():
            results.append({
                'id': loc,
                'name': self.G.nodes[loc]['name'],
                'closeness': closeness[loc],
                'betweenness': betweenness[loc],
                'lat': self.G.nodes[loc]['lat'],
                'lon': self.G.nodes[loc]['lon']
            })
        
        return sorted(results, key=lambda x: x['closeness'], reverse=True)
    
    def optimal_facility_location(self, num_facilities=1):
        """ÛŒØ§ÙØªÙ† Ù…ÙˆÙ‚Ø¹ÛŒØª Ø¨Ù‡ÛŒÙ†Ù‡ Ø¨Ø±Ø§ÛŒ ØªØ³Ù‡ÛŒÙ„Ø§Øª Ø¬Ø¯ÛŒØ¯"""
        # Ø§Ø³ØªÙØ§Ø¯Ù‡ Ø§Ø² Ù…Ø±Ú©Ø²ÛŒØª Ù†Ø²Ø¯ÛŒÚ©ÛŒ Ø¨Ø±Ø§ÛŒ ÛŒØ§ÙØªÙ† Ø¨Ù‡ØªØ±ÛŒÙ† Ù…ÙˆÙ‚Ø¹ÛŒØªâ€ŒÙ‡Ø§
        closeness = nx.closeness_centrality(self.G, distance='distance')
        sorted_locations = sorted(closeness.items(), key=lambda x: x[1], reverse=True)
        
        return [{'id': loc, 'name': self.G.nodes[loc]['name'], 'score': score}
                for loc, score in sorted_locations[:num_facilities]]
    
    def visualize_geographic(self, highlight_path=None, save_path=None):
        """Ù…ØµÙˆØ±Ø³Ø§Ø²ÛŒ Ø¬ØºØ±Ø§ÙÛŒØ§ÛŒÛŒ"""
        plt.figure(figsize=(14, 10))
        
        # Ø§Ø³ØªÙØ§Ø¯Ù‡ Ø§Ø² Ù…Ø®ØªØµØ§Øª Ø¬ØºØ±Ø§ÙÛŒØ§ÛŒÛŒ
        pos = {n: (self.G.nodes[n]['lon'], self.G.nodes[n]['lat']) 
               for n in self.G.nodes()}
        
        # Ø±Ø³Ù… ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§ Ø¨Ø§ Ø¶Ø®Ø§Ù…Øª Ù…Ø¹Ú©ÙˆØ³ ÙØ§ØµÙ„Ù‡
        edges = self.G.edges(data=True)

        edge_widths = [3 * (1 - e[2]['distance']/max_dist) + 0.5 for e in edges]
        
        nx.draw_networkx_edges(self.G, pos, width=edge_widths, 
                               alpha=0.6, edge_color='gray')
        
        # Ø±Ø³Ù… Ú¯Ø±Ù‡â€ŒÙ‡Ø§
        centrality = nx.closeness_centrality(self.G, distance='distance')
        node_sizes = [500 + centrality[n] * 2000 for n in self.G.nodes()]
        node_colors = [centrality[n] for n in self.G.nodes()]
        
        nx.draw_networkx_nodes(self.G, pos, node_size=node_sizes,
                               node_color=node_colors, cmap=plt.cm.YlOrRd,
                               alpha=0.9, edgecolors='black')
        
        # Ø¨Ø±Ú†Ø³Ø¨â€ŒÙ‡Ø§
        labels = {n: self.G.nodes[n]['name'] for n in self.G.nodes()}
        nx.draw_networkx_labels(self.G, pos, labels, font_size=9)
        
        # Ø¨Ø±Ú†Ø³Ø¨ ÙØ§ØµÙ„Ù‡ Ø±ÙˆÛŒ ÛŒØ§Ù„â€ŒÙ‡Ø§
        edge_labels = {(u, v): f"{d['distance']:.0f}km" 
                       for u, v, d in self.G.edges(data=True)}
        nx.draw_networkx_edge_labels(self.G, pos, edge_labels, font_size=7)
        
        # Ù‡Ø§ÛŒÙ„Ø§ÛŒØª Ù…Ø³ÛŒØ±

                     label='Ù…Ø±Ú©Ø²ÛŒØª Ù†Ø²Ø¯ÛŒÚ©ÛŒ', shrink=0.8)
        plt.xlabel('Ø·ÙˆÙ„ Ø¬ØºØ±Ø§ÙÛŒØ§ÛŒÛŒ')
        plt.ylabel('Ø¹Ø±Ø¶ Ø¬ØºØ±Ø§ÙÛŒØ§ÛŒÛŒ')
        plt.title('Ø´Ø¨Ú©Ù‡ Ø¬ØºØ±Ø§ÙÛŒØ§ÛŒÛŒ')

            plt.savefig(save_path, dpi=150, bbox_inches='tight')
        
        plt.show()
